        <td id="L146" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="146"></td>
        <td id="LC146" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">_The background represents the front of the Castle of_ PENTHEUS, _King</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L147" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="147"></td>
        <td id="LC147" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    of Thebes. At one side is visible the sacred Tomb of Semele, a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L148" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="148"></td>
        <td id="LC148" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    little enclosure overgrown with wild vines, with a cleft in the</td>

        <td id="L149" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="149"></td>
        <td id="LC149" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    rocky floor of it from which there issues at times steam or smoke.</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L150" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="150"></td>
        <td id="LC150" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    The God_ DIONYSUS _is discovered alone_.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

        <td id="LC152" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">                  DIONYSUS.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L153" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="153"></td>
        <td id="LC153" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L154" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="154"></td>
        <td id="LC154" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Behold, God&#39;s Son is come unto this land</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L155" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="155"></td>
        <td id="LC155" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of Thebes, even I, Dionysus, whom the brand</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L156" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="156"></td>
        <td id="LC156" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of heaven&#39;s hot splendour lit to life, when she</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L157" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="157"></td>
        <td id="LC157" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Who bore me, Cadmus&#39; daughter Semele,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L158" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="158"></td>
        <td id="LC158" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Died here. So, changed in shape from God to man,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L159" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="159"></td>
        <td id="LC159" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I walk again by Dirce&#39;s streams and scan</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L160" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="160"></td>
        <td id="LC160" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Ismenus&#39; shore. There by the castle side</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L161" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="161"></td>
        <td id="LC161" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I see her place, the Tomb of the Lightning&#39;s Bride,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L162" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="162"></td>
        <td id="LC162" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The wreck of smouldering chambers, and the great</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L163" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="163"></td>
        <td id="LC163" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Faint wreaths of fire undying--as the hate</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L164" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="164"></td>
        <td id="LC164" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Dies not, that Hera held for Semele.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L165" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="165"></td>
        <td id="LC165" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Aye, Cadmus hath done well; in purity</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L166" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="166"></td>
        <td id="LC166" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">He keeps this place apart, inviolate,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L167" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="167"></td>
        <td id="LC167" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">His daughter&#39;s sanctuary; and I have set</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L168" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="168"></td>
        <td id="LC168" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">My green and clustered vines to robe it round.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L169" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="169"></td>
        <td id="LC169" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Far now behind me lies the golden ground</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L170" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="170"></td>
        <td id="LC170" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of Lydian and of Phrygian; far away</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L171" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="171"></td>
        <td id="LC171" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The wide hot plains where Persian sunbeams play,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L172" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="172"></td>
        <td id="LC172" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The Bactrian war-holds, and the storm-oppressed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L173" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="173"></td>
        <td id="LC173" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Clime of the Mede, and Araby the Blest,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L174" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="174"></td>
        <td id="LC174" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And Asia all, that by the salt sea lies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L175" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="175"></td>
        <td id="LC175" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In proud embattled cities, motley-wise</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L176" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="176"></td>
        <td id="LC176" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of Hellene and Barbarian interwrought;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L177" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="177"></td>
        <td id="LC177" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And now I come to Hellas--having taught</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L178" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="178"></td>
        <td id="LC178" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">All the world else my dances and my rite</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L179" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="179"></td>
        <td id="LC179" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of mysteries, to show me in men&#39;s sight</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L180" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="180"></td>
        <td id="LC180" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Manifest God.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L181" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="181"></td>
        <td id="LC181" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">                And first of Hellene lands</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L182" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="182"></td>
        <td id="LC182" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I cry thus Thebes to waken; set her hands</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L183" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="183"></td>
        <td id="LC183" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To clasp my wand, mine ivied javelin,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L184" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="184"></td>
        <td id="LC184" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And round her shoulders hang my wild fawn-skin.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L185" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="185"></td>
        <td id="LC185" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For they have scorned me whom it least beseemed,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L186" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="186"></td>
        <td id="LC186" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Semele&#39;s sisters; mocked my birth, nor deemed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L187" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="187"></td>
        <td id="LC187" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">That Dionysus sprang from Dian seed.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L188" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="188"></td>
        <td id="LC188" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">My mother sinned, said they; and in her need,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L189" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="189"></td>
        <td id="LC189" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">With Cadmus plotting, cloaked her human shame</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L190" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="190"></td>
        <td id="LC190" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">With the dread name of Zeus; for that the flame</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L191" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="191"></td>
        <td id="LC191" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">From heaven consumed her, seeing she lied to God.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L192" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="192"></td>
        <td id="LC192" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Thus must they vaunt; and therefore hath my rod</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L193" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="193"></td>
        <td id="LC193" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">On them first fallen, and stung them forth wild-eyed</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L194" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="194"></td>
        <td id="LC194" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">From empty chambers; the bare mountain side</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L195" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="195"></td>
        <td id="LC195" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Is made their home, and all their hearts are flame.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L196" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="196"></td>
        <td id="LC196" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Yea, I have bound upon the necks of them</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="197"></td>
        <td id="LC197" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The harness of my rites. And with them all</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L198" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="198"></td>
        <td id="LC198" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The seed of womankind from hut and hall</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L199" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="199"></td>
        <td id="LC199" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of Thebes, hath this my magic goaded out.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L200" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="200"></td>
        <td id="LC200" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And there, with the old King&#39;s daughters, in a rout</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L201" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="201"></td>
        <td id="LC201" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Confused, they make their dwelling-place between</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="202"></td>
        <td id="LC202" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The roofless rocks and shadowy pine trees green.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L203" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="203"></td>
        <td id="LC203" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Thus shall this Thebes, how sore soe&#39;er it smart,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L204" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="204"></td>
        <td id="LC204" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Learn and forget not, till she crave her part</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L205" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="205"></td>
        <td id="LC205" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In mine adoring; thus must I speak clear</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L206" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="206"></td>
        <td id="LC206" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To save my mother&#39;s fame, and crown me here</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L207" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="207"></td>
        <td id="LC207" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">As true God, born by Semele to Zeus.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L208" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="208"></td>
        <td id="LC208" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L209" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="209"></td>
        <td id="LC209" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Now Cadmus yieldeth up his throne and use</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L210" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="210"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3009" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3009"></td>
        <td id="LC3009" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">NOTES ON THE BACCHAE</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3010" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3010"></td>
        <td id="LC3010" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3011" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3011"></td>
        <td id="LC3011" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">INTRODUCTORY NOTE</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3012" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3012"></td>
        <td id="LC3012" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3013" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3013"></td>
        <td id="LC3013" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3014" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3014"></td>
        <td id="LC3014" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The _Bacchae_, being from one point of view a religious drama, a kind of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3015" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3015"></td>
        <td id="LC3015" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">&quot;mystery play,&quot; is full of allusions both to the myth and to the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3016" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3016"></td>
        <td id="LC3016" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">religion of Dionysus.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3017" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3017"></td>
        <td id="LC3017" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3018" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3018"></td>
        <td id="LC3018" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">1. The Myth, as implied by Euripides. Semele, daughter of Cadmus, being</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3019" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3019"></td>
        <td id="LC3019" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">loved by Zeus, asked her divine lover to appear to her once in his full</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3020" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3020"></td>
        <td id="LC3020" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">glory; he came, a blaze of miraculous lightning, in the ecstasy of which</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3021" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3021"></td>
        <td id="LC3021" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Semele died, giving premature birth to a son. Zeus, to save this child&#39;s</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3022" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3022"></td>
        <td id="LC3022" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">life and make him truly God as well as Man, tore open his own flesh and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3023" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3023"></td>
        <td id="LC3023" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">therein fostered the child till in due time, by a miraculous and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3024" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3024"></td>
        <td id="LC3024" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">mysterious Second Birth, the child of Semele came to full life as God.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3025" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3025"></td>
        <td id="LC3025" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3026" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3026"></td>
        <td id="LC3026" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">2. The Religion of Dionysus is hard to formulate or even describe, both</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3027" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3027"></td>
        <td id="LC3027" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">because of its composite origins and because of its condition of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3028" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3028"></td>
        <td id="LC3028" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">constant vitality, fluctuation, and development.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3029" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3029"></td>
        <td id="LC3029" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3030" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3030"></td>
        <td id="LC3030" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(_a_) The first datum, apparently, is the introduction from Thrace of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3031" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3031"></td>
        <td id="LC3031" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the characteristic God of the wild northern mountains, a God of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3032" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3032"></td>
        <td id="LC3032" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Intoxication, of Inspiration, a giver of superhuman or immortal life.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3033" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3033"></td>
        <td id="LC3033" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">His worship is superposed upon that of divers old Tree or Vegetation</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3034" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3034"></td>
        <td id="LC3034" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Gods, already worshipped in Greece. He becomes specially the God of the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3035" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3035"></td>
        <td id="LC3035" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Vine. Originally a god of the common folk, despised and unauthorised, he</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3036" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3036"></td>
        <td id="LC3036" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">is eventually so strong as to be adopted into the Olympian hierarchy as</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3037" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3037"></td>
        <td id="LC3037" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the &quot;youngest&quot; of the Gods, son of Zeus. His &quot;Olympian&quot; name, so to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3038" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3038"></td>
        <td id="LC3038" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">speak, is Dionysus, but in his worship he is addressed by numbers of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3039" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3039"></td>
        <td id="LC3039" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">names, more or less mystic and secret--Bromios, Bacchios or Baccheus,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3040" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3040"></td>
        <td id="LC3040" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Iacchos, Eleuthercus, Zagreus, Sabazios, &amp;c. Some of these may be the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3041" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3041"></td>
        <td id="LC3041" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">names of old spirits whom he has displaced; some are his own Thracian</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3042" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3042"></td>
        <td id="LC3042" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">names. Bromos and Sabaja, for instance, seem to have been Thracian names</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3043" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3043"></td>
        <td id="LC3043" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">for two kinds of intoxicating drink. Bacchos means a &quot;wand.&quot; Together</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3044" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3044"></td>
        <td id="LC3044" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">with his many names, he has many shapes, especially appearing as a Bull</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3045" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3045"></td>
        <td id="LC3045" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and a Serpent.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3046" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3046"></td>
        <td id="LC3046" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3047" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3047"></td>
        <td id="LC3047" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(_b_) This religion, very primitive and barbarous, but possessing a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3048" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3048"></td>
        <td id="LC3048" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">strong hold over the emotions of the common people, was seized upon and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3049" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3049"></td>
        <td id="LC3049" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">transfigured by the great wave of religious reform, known under the name</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3050" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3050"></td>
        <td id="LC3050" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of Orphism, which swept over Greece and South Italy in the sixth century</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3051" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3051"></td>
        <td id="LC3051" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">B.C., and influenced the teachings of such philosophers as Pythagoras,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3052" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3052"></td>
        <td id="LC3052" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Aristeas, Empedocles, and the many writers on purification and the world</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3053" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3053"></td>
        <td id="LC3053" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">after death. Orphism may very possibly represent an ancient Cretan</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3054" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3054"></td>
        <td id="LC3054" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">religion in clash or fusion with one from Thrace. At any rate, it was</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L3055" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="3055"></td>
        <td id="LC3055" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">grafted straight upon the Dionysus-worship, and, without rationalising,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
